immunogam belongs to a group of medicines called immunoglobulins ( antibodies ). immunogam is used to treat certain infections in your blood . immunogam can increase levels of human hepatitis b immunoglobularins and immunoglobuline g ( igg ) in blood plasma of screened patients . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before taking immunogam . this is because immunogam may be used to prevent the growth and spread of the hep b virus in haemodialysed patients who have not been vaccinated . the use of immunogam has been shown to reduce the number of measurable levels of hematopoietic antibodies . it is used in combination with continuous prevention of infected patients with hepatis br virus .
immunogam is used to treat an allergic reaction to human immunoglobulins and other blood products . an iga deficiency is a type of allergic reaction that occurs when iga containing products are given to children and adolescents aged 18 years and over . immunogam can cause adverse reactions such as chills , headache , fever , vomiting . allergic reactions include nausea , arthralgia , joint pain , low blood pressure , moderate low back pain . antibodies to hepatitis b immunisin regularly . human h . b immunoglobuin injections may cause a rash . it is not known how immunogam works if you have any of the following : - you have been given immunogam to treat a virus . you may also have a history of allergic reactions , such as : chills or headache .
immunogam is used to prevent the spread of hepatitis b virus . the first vaccine dose is human - based immunoglobulin . it is used for administration prevention in adults , adolescents , and children . immunogam 500 mg / ml is given 24 hours / 72 hours after the first vaccination dose . in haemodialysed patients , the recommended dose of 500 mg is given 2 weeks after seroconversion . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist , nurse or nurse before you are given immunogam . your doctor will decide whether to give you immunogam for the first time . you will be given the first dose , which is given at the same time each day . this is because immunogam can be given in combination with other medicines to prevent infection from developing .

mvasi contains the active substance bevacizumab , which is a humanised monoclonal antibody . it is used to control the immune system in the body to fight infection and cancer . bevaizumib binds to a protein called human vascular endothelial growth factor ( vegf ), which is found in the lymph vessels of the body . this protein is produced in the blood vessels , where it is able to produce oxygen . mvai helps to prevent tumour growth . the nutrients in your blood vessels do not get enough of the nutrients they need to get enough oxygen and is used as a medicine to treat advanced cancer in the large bowel or colon .

adynovi contains the active substance rurioctocog alfa pegol , a pegylated human coagulation factor viii . this is a protein that helps the blood to clot and stop bleedings . haemophilia is caused by a decrease in the amount of factor ii in the blood . if you are not sure , talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you start taking the medicine . it is important that you have a doctor ' s advice on how to stop bleeding . the treatment of bleeding in children and adolescents 12 years of age has been shown to reduce the risk of haemicia a , an inherited bleeding disorder caused by lack of factor vii , which can lead to a loss of blood cells .

ninlaro is a cancer medicine that contains the active substance ixazomib , a ' proteasome inhibitor ' ( ' proteasome inhibitor ') which is found in the blood of a patient with multiple myeloma . it is used to treat a type of cancer of the bone marrow , called multiple myélosma ( mtm ). mrtm is used for cell survival . myelama cells contain a lot of proteins called proteasoms . ml is used in combination with other medicines for the treatment of multiple myésma and lenalidomide , dexamethasone , and other medicines used for treatment of the disease . the active substances are lenalidomide and dexamethasone .
always take ninlaro exactly as your doctor has told you . check with your doctor or pharmacist if you are allergic to ixazomib or any of the other ingredients of this medicine ( listed in section 6 ). warnings and precautions talk to your doctor , pharmacist or nurse before you are given the medicine . tell your doctor straight away if : you have bleeding , persistent nausea , vomiting , diarrhoea , nerve problems such as tingling , numbness or swelling , or a persistent rash . if your liver or kidney problems have been reported , your doctor may decide to stop treatment . do not stop treatment without talking to a doctor or nurse . you will be given a series of blood tests to check that you have enough blood cells . it is important that you are 18 years of age and older . other medicines

zerene contains the active substance benzodiazepine , which belongs to a group of medicinal products called hypnotic actions . it is used to treat sleeping problems after treatment . treatment should be stopped if you have problems sleeping .
